 sansad kaa bajet satr 23 farvari, mangalvaar ko shuru hone ja rahaa he
 The 2016-17 General Budget will be presented in the Lok Sabha on next Monday, February 29
 is bich yadhyapi bajet kii taiyaariyon main north blaak (vitt mantralay) main paramparaagat gopneeyata barti ja rahi he, par is saal aisa pehla mauka he jab vitt mantralay main sachivon ne aam bajet 2016-17 kii disha kaa sanket dene ke liye you-tub kaa sahaara liya he
 Using its own youtube channel, the Ministry has shown the importance of the budget
 mantralay ne bajet ko prastut karne ke liye vitt mantri dwaara bajet patron ko chamade ke ek brifces main le jane kii paripati ko bhi pradarshit kiya he
 Generally, the entry of journalists and general public in the concerned part of the North Block, which is preparing for the budget, is stopped from the beginning of January
 iske saath hi north block main aane vaali or yahaan se baahar jane vaali har cheez ko vishesh eks-re scan se guzaar kar us par paini najar rakhi jaataa he
 Also, powerful mobile phone jammer devices are installed, so that no information can be excluded from mobile phone calls
 varisht adhikariyon or prakriya main shaamil karmchaariyon ke karyaalayon main internet conection band kar die jate hai or north block kii bajet shakha ek waar-room kii tarah kaam karne lagati he
 The highest level of security measures in North Block remain in force until the budget is presented in the Lok Sabha
 is kshetra kii suraksha main khufia karyaalay (ibi), dilli police or siaisef sabhi shaamil rahete hai
 This time the final phase of budget preparation started on Friday with the pudding ceremony
 isamen aam bajet ke dastavejon kii chapai kii prakriya shuru hoti he
 There is no worship in this ceremony
 jetali or is bajet kii taiyaariyon se jude adhikari north block ke basament main sthit printing press main ekatra hue or ek-duusare ko shubhakamanaayen dete hue halava baanta
 With this, the countdown for the budget day started
 bajet aamtaur par farvari ke antim din pesh kiya jaataa he or is saal farvari kaa aakhri din 29 farvari, somvaar ko pad rahaa he
 a few weeks later, assembly elections are due in states like West Bengal, Kerala and Assam
 in sabhi dastavejon kii suraksha ek 'nila jacket' karata he
 It is also called blue jacket because it contains significant numbers for the budget
 mantralay kaa sanyukt sachiv (bajet) iskaa prabharee hota he or vah kisi ko bhi yahaan tak ki vitt mantri ko bhi ise north block se baahar le jane nahin detaa
 During the entire budget-making process, only a few officers of the Ministry are able to see this document
 vitt mantri kaa bhaashan, bajet pesh hone se kuch ghante pehle hi taiyaar kiya jaataa he
 This time budget is important in the sense that Jaitley has to accelerate the growth rate and solve the problems of low investment in the country
 iske saath hi un par rajkoshiya ghaataa or rajasav ghate par bhi niyantran karne kii jimmedaari he
 With limited resources, Jaitley is also tasked with keeping the middle class happy and addressing issues in areas such as agriculture and infrastructure
 kai log bajet main badi ghoshnaaon kii ummid nahin kar rahe hai, lekin aarthik sudhaaron ke liye visheshkar tex ke morche par ek ruparekha pesh kiye jane kii ummid jarur he, jisase niveshkon kaa vishwaas behaal kiya ja sake
 From 1947 (when the first budget was presented on November 26, 1947) to 1950, the printing of the budget document was done in Rashtrapati Bhavan, but after the budget was leaked in 1950, the printing of the government was changed to a government press tax on Minto Road
 Given
 tippaniyan However, since 1980 the North Block's basement has become a permanent place for printing
 yah bajet press purna vaataanukoolit he or aadhunik printing mashiinon se las he
 After the pudding ceremony, 100 employees are taken to the basement of the North Block, where there are two printing presses
 vahaan unhen sampurna prakriya puri hone tak rakhaa jaataa he or koi bhi bahari vyakti unase sampark nahin kar saktaa
 These people are involved in printing, proof reading and translation work

 apane khud ke you-tub channel kaa upyog karte hue mantralay ne bajet kaa mahatv darshaya hai
 The ministry has also demonstrated the pattern of carrying the budget papers in a leather briefcase by the finance minister to present the budget
 aamtaur par bajet kii taiyaari main lagi north block ke sambandhit hisse main janvari ke shuru se hi patrakaron evam aam janata kaa pravesh band kar diya jaataa he
 With this, everything coming in and going out of North Block is subjected to special X-ray scans and it is monitored closely
 saath hi shaktishaalee mobile phone jaimar yantra laga die jate hai, taaki mobile phone kol se kisi soochna ko baahar na kiya ja sake
 Internet connections are closed in the offices of senior officers and employees involved in the process, and the budget branch of North Block functions as a war room
 loksabhaa main bajet pesh hone tak north block main suraksha ke ucchtam str ke upaay lagu rahete hai
 The Security Office (IB), Delhi Police and CISF are all involved in the security of the region
 is baar bajet kii taiyaari kaa antim charan shuukravaar ko halava samaaroh ke saath shuru ho gaya
 In this, the process of printing the documents of the general budget begins
 is samaaroh main koi puja-archana nahin hoti
 Jaitley and the officials involved with the preparations for this budget gathered in the printing press located in the basement of North Block and distributed halwa, greeting each other
 iske saath hi bajet ke din ke liye ulti ginati shuru ho gai
 The budget is usually presented on the last day of February and the last day of February this year is falling on 29 February, Monday
 iske kuch saptaah baad pashchim bengal, kerala or assam jaise rajyon main vidhansabha chunaav hone hai
 All these documents are protected by a 'blue jacket'
 ise nila jacket isliye bhi kehete hai, kyonki isamen bajet ke liye mahatvapurn sankhya hote hai
 The joint secretary (budget) of the ministry is in charge of this and does not let anyone, even the finance minister, take it out of the North Block
 bajet banane kii sampurna prakriya ke dauraan mantralay ke kuch hi adhikari is dastavej ko dekh pate hai
 The Finance Minister's speech is prepared a few hours before the Budget is presented
 is baar kaa bajet is lihaaj se ahm he ki jetali ko vruddhi dar main teji lani he or desh main kam nivesh ko lekar aa rahi samasyaon kaa samaadhaan karnaa he
 Along with this, they also have the responsibility to control the fiscal deficit and revenue deficit
 simit sansadhano ke saath jetali par madhyam varg ko khush rakhane evam krishi va dhanchaagat jaise kshetron ke muddon kaa samaadhaan karne kaa bhi jimmaa he
 Many are not expecting major announcements in the budget, but a framework is expected to be introduced for economic reforms, especially on the tax front, to restore investor confidence
 varsh 1947 (jab 26 november, 1947 ko pehla bajet pesh kiya gaya tha) se lekar 1950 tak bajet dastavej kii chapai raashtrapati bhawan main hua karti thi, lekin 1950 main bajet li hone ke baad chapai kaa sthaan badalakar minto road sthit ek sarkaar press kar diya gaya
 The comments haalanki, 1980 se north block kaa basament chapai ke liye ek sthaayee jagah ban gaya he
 This budget press is fully air conditioned and equipped with modern printing machines
 halava samaaroh ke baad 100 karmchaariyon ko north block ke basament main le jaaya jaataa he, jahaan do printing press hai
 There they are kept till the entire process is completed and no outsider can contact them

 sweep shot kii kami khal rahi thiaaj kii cricket ke daur main jahaan ballebaaj sweep shot se kahin aage pedal sweep, reverse sweep or switch hint kaa lagaataar prayog kar rahe hai vahaan inke basic yani ki sweep shot kaa apni batting se baahar hona viraat ko bahut khal rahaa tha

 ' is baat kaa saral hindi main anuwaad karen to vah sarkaar, jo apane nagarikon kii buniyadi jaruratein puri karne kaa kaam sunishchit kare
 The immediate reason for thinking about this is the manifesto issued in Bihar elections before us and the promises made by sensational announcements in the Lok Sabha elections just a year and a half ago
 apni charchaa main ek yah tathy or jod liya jaae ki loktantric chunavi raajnneeti main ab pehle jaisaa jamaana nahin rahaa
 What are the conditions of the country or state, and the conditions of their citizens, what is the first to fulfill their needs, and in what amount of time it is our capacity to complete it
 
 
 ? is sabakaa hisaab lagaakar chalanaa raajnneeti ke gujarey jamaane kii baat he
 In a new era of economic dominance, this is not the time to fulfill the needs of the people, but to devise political strategies according to the desire of the people
 is baat ko kah sakane kaa aadhaar yaa saboot yah he ki chunavi ranneeti main naveenatam prabandhan praudyogiki kaa istemaal sabake saamne he
 In particular, all knowledge, science and technology which is helpful in marketing or marketing or selling goods is being used in electoral strategy
 lekin yahaan ek bahut badi or baarik baat yah he ki aadhunik prabandhan praudyogiki ne upabhoktaaon kii aavashyaktaaon kii purti nahin, balki unamem ichchhaaon ko paidaa karne ke upaay dhunde hai
 In the current election manifestos of Bihar, the number of promises that generate a lot of desire among voters is worth counting
 haa, loksabhaa chunaav ke dauraan kaala dhan waapas laane or karodon rojgaar paidaa kar dene ke vaadon kii pole khulne ke baad aa rahi baari dikkat se yah sabak jarur liya gaya he ki philhal is prajati ke vaadon ko khulkar karne se abhi bachakar chalaa jaae
 For example, in the promise of distributing laptops and scooties to college children, these numbers have been written in such a way, that it does not look like how it will happen, and it does not seem so small that everyone will get this stuff
 11 karod aabaadi vaale bihar main 28 saal se kam umr ke yuvaaon kii sankhya dhai karod he, jinamein ladkiyaan sava karod hai
 After being able to run Scooty or create a desire for Scooty, the number of such girls is more than 50 lakhs
 ek ghoshnaptr main paanch hajaar skuti kaa zikr he
 If God does not become a banker to distribute crispy scooters, will there not be a lottery-like situation? 
 
 ? vaise sirf medhaavi ladakiyon ko hi skuti baatane kaa pointer halke se laga jarur diya gaya he, lekin prachaar kaa tarika aisa he ki sabhi main aakanksha yaa ichha kaa nirmaan kar diya gaya he

 ? ghoshnaptr ke dheron vaadon ko ek-ek karke dekhnaa shuru karenge to bihar ke chunaav kii taarikh hi nikal jaaegi
 So, let us briefly mention the formula which we can check the credibility of any manifesto
 yah formula vishwastareey prabandh-patu vaigyanikon kii shodhaparak khoj he or iskaa istemaal udyog vyapaar kii yojana banaate samay duniya ke viksit deshon main hota he
 In the field of business, it is taught in the famous management institutes of the world under the name Target Management
 angreji main 'gol management' naam se padhaaye jane vaale is paath main paanch bindu hai, jinke pehle angreji akshar ko lekar ek parichit shabd 'smart' ban gaya - es em e aar tii

 Book Name: Modi live Author Name: Sanjay Dwivedi Publisher: Media Discussion Price: Rs 25 for the 2014 General Elections and Modi These two main points and many doubts related to every point and their solutions are all included in 'modi live'
 desh kii swadhinata se lekar 2014 tak ke chunaavon tak ke prayek ghatnakram, tatkaaleen raajnneeti, rajnatik dalon kii karypranali sabhi ko bakhubi ubhaara he sanjay dvivedi ne pustak 'modi live' main
 Expectations of the public mind from Jan Nayak, 2014 elections, Nayak's magnetic personality, his style of work, awareness of the people, the politics of turn-taking and the power of democracy are all expressed in a very interesting and effective manner in 'modi live'
 modi anayas hi janata ke nayak nahin bane balki ghatnakram se sanjay dvivedi ne yah siddh kiya he
 Sanjay has been keeping an eye on every development
 janata ke saath sidhaa judaav or unke man main ummiido ke puraa hone kaa vishwaas jagaanaa aasaan nahin hota
 The author has made it clear from the example of Modi that if the hero has insensitivity with the people in the democracy, then it does not take long to turn the power
 modi janata se nirantar jude rahe or yahi judaav unhen vijayi bana gaya
 Modi's charismatic personality and the right use of media were not enough to make Modi a hero
 modi ke saath keval sapane nahin the balki unhen saakaar karne ke liye drudh sankalp the or suniyojit kaaryastylee bhi
 Sanjay Dwivedi has a special view on BJP, Sangh and Modi
 koi bhi ghatnakram sanjay kii pakad se achoota nahin rahaa he
 Sanjay has also commented on the failure of Congress and the reasons for that failure
 sangh or bijepi kaa judaav or sangh ke hi dwaara narendra modi ko nayak ke rup main prastut karnaa anayas nahin balki badi kushalta se sanjay ne yah darshaya he ki nayak vahi hota he jiske paas doordarshita hoti he or jan-jan kii samasyaon ke samaadhan bhi
 This was the reason that the historic victory of the BJP, not the BJP, made the government with an absolute majority in the name of Modi, because Modi is encouraged to show a new and meaningful tax out of the box
 lekhak sanjay dvivedi ne desh ke vibhaajan se lekar 2009 tak ke chunaav parinaam or unke kaaran va 2014 ke chunaav main bijepi kii jeet kaa nishpaksh vishleshan kiya he
 Sanjay has clarified that victory is not achieved by uniting all political parties against a particular person, but by creating trust in the heart of the people
 sansadeey loktantr ko bhi lekhak sanjay dwidi ne bakhubi paribhaashit kiya he
 Whereas protests were limited during Pandit Nehru, today, political opposition is seen as criticism and indecent behavior is seen in Parliament
 lekhak sanjay dvivedi ne loktantr kii shakti ko bhi ujagar kiya he ki anek rajnatik dalon ke baavjood bhi ham safal hai or jan-jan kii aawaaj ko darkinar nahin kiya ja saktaa
 Sanjay has given special emphasis on unity in speech and deeds because this creates confidence in the public's mind
 media kii sahabhaagita ko lekhak ne vishesh mahatv diya he
 According to the author, today's time is really mediay time
 media kii hi badaulat ham aaj har raajnneetijna ko jaanate or pahachaanate hai
 If the 2014 election was historic, it was through the media
 modi ne bhi apane ek saakshaatkaar main yah spasht kiya he, 'yadi soshal media naa hota to aam aadmi kii creativity kaa pataa nahin chalata
 Sanjay Dwivedi has been closely watching every incident of the election campaign
 ek jaagruk or jindadil patrkaar banakar sanjay saamne aae hai

 Groundwater sources and rivers have caught the attention of policy makers of the country amid shortage of water
 ye jal strot ab radar par hai
 For centuries, lakes, ponds, baoli and other natural and man-made water sources have been providing water for drinking, domestic use and agriculture
 ye jalstrot bhoojal str badhaate hai
 Also reduce the possibility of floods in cities
 aise jalsroton par atikaraman kii vajah se hi kai shaharon ko flash flud kaa shikaar hona padaa
 During the last decade and a half, Mumbai in 2005, Uttarakhand in 2013, Jammu and Kashmir in 2014 and Chennai in 2015 have suffered similar flash floods
 agar ham niti ayog kii siforeeshon par dhyaan den to jalsroton ke punarutthan or prabandhan par zyada jor dene kii jarurat he
 Because by the year 2020, groundwater in 21 major cities of the country including Delhi, Hyderabad and Bengaluru will be exhausted
 isse 10 karod log prabhavit honge
 Due to uncontrolled urbanization, water from cities and villages is rapidly ending
 ye ham din pratidin dekhte bhi hai or vibhinn research report main padhate bhi hai
 The biggest reason for the bad condition of the water resources is the move from encroachment, garbage dumps, sewerage, industrial waste, construction debris and community use of water to personal use
 teji se gaayab hote jalsrothadesh ke vibhinn rajyon se jalstrot teji se gaayab ho rahe hai
 According to the Third Minor Irrigation (MI) census 2000-01, there were 556,601 streams in the country, which decreased to 523,816 in the fourth Minor Irrigation (MI) census in 2006-07
 yani 32,785 jalstrot ghat gaye
 Of these 523,816 waters, 80,128 (15%) were left unused
 aise jalstrot karnataka, rajasthan, andhra pradesh, tamilnadu, uttarakhand or gujarat main zyada hai
 The Minor Irrigation (MI) census does not show an accurate picture of the entire country as it is limited to rural areas only
 2013-14 main paanchvaan miner irigation (MI) sensos hua tha lekin jalsroton kaa data jari nahin kiya gaya
 a drawback to the Minor Irrigation (MI) census is that the statistics of all the water resources of the states are there but it is not known which source is not in use
 saath hi yah bhi nahin bataaya gaya he ki kis jalstrot ko kitna nuksaan hua he or kyon
 Due to this, the work of resurrection of water bodies is not being done
 jal sansaadhan sambandhi sansadeey sthaayee samiti ne 2016 or 2017 main shahari or gramin ilaakon par do report taiyaar kii he
 In this, many questions were asked to the state governments regarding the sources of water, but the state governments did not give any answer to the Center
 is vajah se centre sarkaar 2019-20 main hone vaale chathe miner irigation (MI) sensos kii shuruyaat nahin ho paa rahi he
 Annoyed by this attitude of the state governments, the Parliamentary Standing Committee on Water Resources said that there is a need to conduct a survey regarding the immediate water resources in the country
 agar yah jald nahin kiya gaya to jalsroton ke saath utpann ho rahi samasyaon kaa samaadhaan khojna mushkil hoga
 The Ministry of Water Resources also expressed concern over the dwindling water resources
 desh main sabhi jalsroton kii sankhya to satellite masping se pataa chal jaati he
 But the Parliamentary Standing Committee on Water Resources has expressed concern that the number of water resources and their uses is not of any use until solutions are found on the basis of them
 jalsroton ke liye repere, rinovations or restauration skimcendre sarkaar ne 2005 main jalsroton ke repere, rinovations or restauration (RRR) skim launch kii thi
 It was planned to increase storage capacity, ground water and drinking water
 iske tahat paaramparik jalsroton ko sangrakshit karne, unka jalastr badhaane, tanks storage kshamta badhaane, bhoojal str main ijapha karnaa aadi shaamil tha
 But after the Parliamentary Standing Committee on Water Resources objected to the bad condition of the watershed, there is a need to revisit the repair, renovation and restoration (RRR) scheme
 sanyukt raashtra ke vishwa jal vikaas report 2018 ke anusaar duniya ke sabhi deshon ko paaramparik tareekon ko apanaakar prakritik jalsroton ko bachaane ke apil kii thi
 Two big examples were given in this
 pehla rajasthan ke alvar jile main bharat ke waterman kahe jane vaale rajendra singh kii yojana
 In which he raised the water level by creating small rain water harvesting structures in 1000 drought affected villages
 isaki vajah se in gaanvon ke krishi upaj main 20 se 80 fisadi kaa ijapha hua
 At the same time 33 percent of the forests also increased
 doosraa udhaaharan jordan kaa tha
 Where traditional land management system HIMA has been introduced
 yahaan jameen ko uske prakritik haal par chhod diya gaya taaki vah khud-ba-khud sudhaar laa sake
 Also, such plants were planted which are financially strengthening the country
 jordan ne jarka river basin ke prakritik sansadhano ke bachaane ke liye bhi yahi formula lagaaya
 There are many schemes in the country that promote traditional water management but this is not the case with the Repair, Renovation and Restoration (RRR) scheme
 jal sansaadhan sambandhi sansadeey sthaayee samiti ne kaha tha ki RRR skim ke jariye nae jalstrot bhi banaae jaaen taaki khatm ho rahe puraane jalsroton kii kami ko puraa kiya ja sake
 States like Madhya Pradesh, Telangana, Arunachal Pradesh, Rajasthan, Mizoram, Tripura and Odisha have created new tanks, check dams like water resources under mnrega-like schemes
 lekin jal sansaadhan mantralay ne sansadeey samiti kii sifarish ko khaarij kar diya
